Do not collect personal/sensitive data.\n\n### Quick Start\n\n**Docker (Recommended):**\n```bash\ndocker-compose up --build\n```\n\n**Local Development:**\n```bash\n./scripts/setup.sh && python3 backend/python_core/automation.py --once --target demo\n```\n\n**Termux Run:**\n```bash\nbash scripts/run.sh\n```\n\n### Project Structure\n\n```\nHEX-Control-Nexus/\n‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ backend/\n‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ python_core/        # Core automation, scrapers, API clients\n‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ java_service/       # Spring Boot microservice\n‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ node_webhooks/      # Webhook listener, Puppeteer tasks\n‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ web_dashboard/          # Frontend dashboard\n‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ config/                 # Configuration files\n‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ database/               # SQLite database\n‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ scripts/                # Setup and run scripts\n‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ tests/                  # Unit tests\n‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Dockerfile              # Multi-stage Dockerfile\n‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ docker-compose.yml      # Services orchestration\n```\n\n### Features\n\n1. **Web Scraping (Python)**\n   - Static: requests + BeautifulSoup\n   - JS pages: Puppeteer integration\n   - Rate-limiting, user-agent rotation\n   - robots.txt compliance\n\n2. **API Automation**\n   - Python async client (httpx/aiohttp)\n   - Java synchronous endpoints\n   - Retries with exponential backoff\n\n3. **Browser Automation**\n   - Node.js Puppeteer tasks\n   - Screenshot-on-error\n   - Remote WebDriver support\n\n4. **Webhooks & Triggers**\n   - Node.js webhook listener\n   - Job queue with status tracking\n\n5. **Scheduler & Runner**\n   - CLI interface with multiple options\n   - Termux-friendly runner script\n\n6. **Notifications**\n   - Telegram, Email, Slack/Discord support\n\n7. **Monitoring & Logging**\n   - Structured JSON logs\n   - Real-time dashboard with WebSocket\n   - Health and metrics endpoints\n\n### Configuration\n\nThe main configuration file is `config/config.json`. You can define scraping targets, rate limits, and other settings.\n\n### Safety & Legal\n\nUse responsibly. Always check robots.txt and website terms. Do not collect or store personal or sensitive data without permission.\n\n### Testing\n\nRun tests with:\n```bash\n# Python tests\npython -m pytest tests/\n\n# Node.js tests\ncd backend/node_webhooks && npm test\n```\n\n### Deployment\n\n1. **Docker Deployment:**\n   ```bash\n   ./scripts/deploy_docker.sh\n   ```\n\n2. **Manual Deployment:**\n   - Run setup script: `./scripts/setup.sh`\n   - Start services: `./scripts/run.sh`\n\n### Adding New Targets\n\n1. Edit `config/config.json`\n2. Add a new target object with required fields\n3. Run the automation engine\n\n### Enabling Telegram Notifications\n\n1. Create a Telegram bot via @BotFather\n2. Get your chat ID\n3. Update `.env` with credentials\n4. Enable in `config/config.json`\n\n### License\n\nThis project is licensed under the MIT License - see the LICENSE file for details.\n\n---\n\n*HEX Control Nexus - Multi-Language Automation Hub*\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}

jobs table\nfunction updateJobsTable() {\n    if (jobs.length === 0) {\n        jobsTableBody.innerHTML = \'<tr><td colspan="6" style="text-align: center;">No active jobs</td></tr>\';\n        return;\n    }\n\n    jobsTableBody.innerHTML = jobs.map(job => `\n        <tr>\n            <td>${job.id}</td>\n            <td>${job.task}</td>\n            <td>${job.target}</td>\n            <td><span class="status-badge ${job.status}">${job.status}</span></td>\n            <td>${new Date(job.createdAt).toLocaleTimeString()}</td>\n            <td>\n                <button class="btn            const data = JSON.parse(event.data);\n            handleWebSocketMessage(data);\n        } catch (error) {\n            addLogEntry(\'error\', `Failed to parse WebSocket message: ${error.message}`);\n        }\n    };\n    \n    ws.onclose = function() {\n        addLogEntry(\'warning\', \'WebSocket connection closed. Web Scraping (Python)\n- Static scraping with requests + BeautifulSoup\n- Dynamic pages with Puppeteer integration\n- Pagination support\n- Rate limiting and user-agent rotation\n- robots.txt compliance\n- Multiple storage options (CSV, JSONL, SQLite)\n\n### 2. API Automation\n- Async HTTP client (httpx/aiohttp)\n- Retry logic with exponential backoff\n- Circuit breaker pattern\n- Authentication management\n- ETL pipeline examples\n\n### 3. Browser Automation\n- Puppeteer tasks for complex interactions\n- Screenshot capture on error\n- Remote WebDriver support for Termux\n- Headless and GUI modes\n\n### 4. Webhooks & Triggers\n- REST endpoint for external triggers\n- Job queue management\n- Real-time status updates via WebSocket\n\n### 5. Scheduler & Runner\n- CLI interface with multiple options\n- Daemon mode for continuous operation\n- Configurable targets and schedules\n- Dry-run capability\n\n### 6. Notifications\n- Telegram bot integration\n- Email notifications\n- Slack/Discord webhook support\n\n### 7. Monitoring & Logging\n- Structured JSON logging\n- Real-time dashboard\n- Health and metrics endpoints\n- WebSocket log streaming\n\n### 8. Security & Persistence\n- Environment-based secrets management\n- SQLite job persistence\n- Graceful shutdown handling\n- Retry policies\n\n## üìã Configuration\n\n### Sample Target Configuration\n```json\n{\n  "targets": [\n    {\n      "name": "quotes_static",\n      "mode": "static",\n      "base_url": "http://quotes.toscrape.com",\n      "start_paths": ["/"],\n      "selectors": {\n        "item": ".quote",\n        "fields": {"text": ".text", "author": ".author", "tags": ".tags .tag"}\n      },\n      "pagination": {"next_selector": ".next a"},\n      "storage": {"type": "sqlite", "path": "database/hex_data.db"}\n    }\n  ]\n}\n```\n\n## üß™ Testing\n```bash\n# Run Python tests\npython -m pytest tests/test_web_scraper.py -v\n\n# Run Node.js tests\ncd backend/node_webhooks && npm test\n\n# Run all tests\nmake test\n```\n\n## üê≥ Docker Deployment\n```bash\n# Build and run with docker-compose\n./scripts/deploy_docker.sh\n\n# Or manually\ndocker-compose up --build\n```\n\n## üì± Termux Usage\n```bash\n# Print banner\ncat scripts/banner.txt && echo -e "\\e[92mH\\e[91mE\\e[92mX\\e[0m"\n\n# Run automation loop\nbash scripts/run.sh\n```\n\n## üìä Dashboard Access\n- **Web Dashboard**: http://localhost:8000\n- **Node.js Webhook...\n The full message content is stored at /workspace/summarized_conversations/original_conversation_1762327641_5790.txt'}

Do not collect personal or sensitive data without permission.\n\n---\n\n## üìã Project Overview\n\n**HEX Control Nexus** is an advanced multi-language automation hub designed for web scraping, API automation, browser automation, and webhook management. Built with a focus on ethical use and compliance, this system integrates Python, Java, and Node.js components to provide a comprehensive automation solution.\n\n### üîß Key Features\n\n- **Web Scraping**: Static (requests/BeautifulSoup) and dynamic (Puppeteer) scraping with robots.txt compliance\n- **API Automation**: Async HTTP client with retry logic and circuit breaker pattern\n- **Browser Automation**: Puppeteer tasks with screenshot capabilities\n- **Webhooks**: Node.js webhook listener with job queue management\n- **Scheduler**: CLI interface with daemon mode and configurable targets\n- **Notifications**: Telegram, email, Slack/Discord support\n- **Monitoring**: Structured JSON logging, real-time dashboard, health/metrics endpoints\n- **Security**: Environment-based secrets management, graceful shutdown, retry policies\n\n---\n\n## üöÄ Quick Start\n\n### Docker Deployment (Recommended)\n\n```bash\ndocker-compose up --build\n```\n\n### Local Development\n\n```bash\n./scripts/setup.sh && python3 backend/python_core/automation.py --once --target demo\n```\n\n### Termux Environment\n\n```bash\nbash scripts/run.sh\n```\n\n---\n\n## üìÅ Project Structure\n\n```\nHEX-Control-Nexus/\n‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ backend/\n‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ python_core/\n‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ java_service/\n‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ node_webhooks/\n‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ web_dashboard/\n‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ
